msg:Tianmu Lake Hotel is located at No. 588 Yingbin Avenue, Tianmu Lake Tourism Resort, Changzhou City, Jiangsu Province. It is a five-star hotel with Tianmu Lake in front of the hotel. The hotel has a good environment and is clean. The lake view room we stayed in faces the scenery of Tianmu Lake. The air is good. Standing on the balcony of the room, I feel comfortable looking at the landscape lake.
Tianmu Lake Fisherman's Head Soup, which was first created by the catering depar**ent of Tianmu Lake Hotel, is a major feature of the hotel. This time I came here to taste it. The fisherman's head soup tastes good, and I also tasted other varieties of dishes. The restaurant waiters are thoughtful and worthy of praise.
The self-service breakfast restaurant in the hotel has a good environment, facing Tianmu Lake, with a variety of breakfast varieties, and Western-style snacks are worth tasting. The waiters are enthusiastic and caring for the elderly and help them deliver meals to the table, which is worthy of praise.

The hotel is old, but the maintenance is OK. The second-floor platform is used to transform into a children's play area and a small garden, and the gym equipment is also very complete.

The only thing that is not so good is the sound insulation. The sound of rinsing in the bathroom is clear in the room, and the sound in the corridor is also clearly heard.
